Accessibility digest

Requesterpool@jpdev.pro

Score763
Tested byTestaro, procedure ts24
Scored byTestilo, procedure tsp24
Digested byTestilo, procedure tdp24

Introduction

This is a digest of results from a battery of accessibility Tests.

The battery includes 1353 automated accessibility tests drawn from ten different packages: Alfa, Axe, Continuum, Equal Access, HTML CodeSniffer, Nu Html Checker, QualWeb, Tenon, Testaro, and WAVE.

These tests were run on the web page named above and gave the page a score of 763, where 0 would be perfect.

Issue summary

Special issues

log: Score 235. This is based on the amount of browser error logging and miscellaneous logging during the tests.

preventions: Score 100. This is based on tests that the page did not allow to be run. That impedes accessibility progress and risks interfering with tools that users with disabilities need.

Classified issues

Issue overflowHidden

WCAG: 1.4.4

Score: 54

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package qualWeb, test QW-ACT-R40, score 52 (Zoomed text node is clipped by a CSS overflow declaration)

Issue focusIndication

WCAG: 2.4.7

Score: 45

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package testaro, test focInd, score 11 (Focused element displays no or a nostandard focus indicator)
  • Package qualWeb, test QW-ACT-R62, score 39 (Element in the sequential focus order has no visible focus)

Issue linkIndication

WCAG: 1.3.3

Score: 30

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package testaro, test linkUl, score 28 (Non-underlined adjacent links)

Issue targetSize

WCAG: 2.5.5

Score: 29

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package tenon, test 152, score 27 (Actionable element is smaller than the minimum required size)

Issue iframeTitleBad

WCAG: 4.1.2

Score: 20

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package axe, test frame-title-unique, score 2 (Frame title attribute is not unique)
  • Package htmlcs, test e:AAA.2_4_1.H64.1, score 16 (iframe element has no non-empty title attribute)
  • Package qualWeb, test QW-ACT-R10, score 2 (iframe elements with identical accessible names have different purposes)

Issue linkForcesNewWindow

WCAG: 3.2.5

Score: 20

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package tenon, test 218, score 18 (Link opens in a new window without user control)

Issue imageNoText

WCAG: 1.1.1

Score: 16

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package axe, test image-alt, score 4 (Image has no text alternative)
  • Package continuum, test 89, score 4 (img element has no mechanism that allows an accessible name to be calculated)
  • Package htmlcs, test e:AAA.1_1_1.H37, score 8 (img element has no alt attribute)
  • Package wave, test e:alt_missing, score 4 (Text alternative is missing)
  • Package wave, test e:alt_spacer_missing, score 4 (Spacer image has no text alternative)

Issue linkNoText

WCAG: 2.4.4

Score: 16

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package axe, test link-name, score 6 (Link has no discernible text)
  • Package continuum, test 237, score 8 (a element has no mechanism that allows an accessible name value to be calculated)
  • Package htmlcs, test w:AAA.4_1_2.H91.A.Empty, score 1 (a element has an id attribute but no href attribute or text)
  • Package wave, test e:alt_link_missing, score 4 (Linked image has no text alternative)
  • Package tenon, test 57, score 4 (Link has no text inside it)
